</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/catch_all_p2.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/catch_all_p2.png" alt="catch-all-p2" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Wizard Page 3 - "Provider Configuration"</h4><a id="user-content-wizard-page-3---provider-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Wizard Page 3 - &quot;Provider Configuration&quot;" href="#wizard-page-3---provider-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Name: <code>Provider for Domain Wide Forward Auth Catch All</code></li>
<li>Authentication Flow: <code>empty</code><br>
<em>This is user choice, I recommend getting the basics setup and THEN modifying authentication flow for the catch all</em></li>
<li>Authorization Flow: <code>default-provider-authorization-explicit-consent (Authorize Application)</code><br>
<em>Explicit requires user interaction aka clicking a button to continue versus implicit which is just trust</em></li>
<li>External Host: <code>https://authentik.domain.tld</code></li>
<li>Cookie Domain: <code>domain.tld</code></li>
<li>Token Validity: <code>hours=24</code><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/catch_all_p3.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/catch_all_p3.png" alt="catch-all-p3" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">When all is done, you should have success.  If not, carefully review the previous settings.  You most likely forgot <code>https://</code> in front of <code>authentik.domain.tld</code><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/wizard_success.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/wizard_success.png" alt="wizard-success" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Embedded Outpost (Domain Wide)</h4><a id="user-content-embedded-outpost-domain-wide" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Embedded Outpost (Domain Wide)" href="#embedded-outpost-domain-wide"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Navigate to the Outposts screen and edit the Embedded Outpost:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Applications</li>
<li>Outposts</li>
<li>Edit the Embedded Outpost</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/edit_embed.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/edit_embed.png" alt="edit-embed" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Notice how the above picture has <code>Providers</code> empty?</p>
<p dir="auto">Update the Outpost to have the <code>Domain Wide Forward Auth Catch All</code> in <code>Selected Applications</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><em><strong>BEFORE Adding</strong></em><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/before_add.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/before_add.png" alt="before-add" style="max-width: 100%;"></a><br>
<em><strong>AFTER Adding</strong></em><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/after_add.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/after_add.png" alt="after-add" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Now the Embedded Outpost shows the <code>Provider</code> for the Catch All rule instead of it being empty/blank:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/updated_provider.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/updated_provider.png" alt="updated-provider" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Domain Wide / Catch All Test/Validation</h3><a id="user-content-domain-wide--catch-all-testvalidation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Domain Wide / Catch All Test/Validation" href="#domain-wide--catch-all-testvalidation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Now that the catch all rule is in place, validate it using the already running <code>whoami-catchall</code> container created:</p>
<p dir="auto">Navigate to <code>whoami-catchall.domain.tld</code> and it will immediately redirect you to Authentik to login:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/fa_splash.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/fa_splash.png" alt="fa-splash" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Sign in with your username or email address initially created. After inputting username &amp; password, it should show you the "Redirecting" screen prior to actual redirection:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/whoami-all.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/whoami-all.png" alt="whoami-all" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>X-Authentik-Meta-App</code> will contain information about the specific Application used to get here. Notice that this matches the <code>slug</code> previously created.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="X-Authentik-Meta-App: domain-wide-forward-auth-catch-all"><pre><span class="pl-ent">X-Authentik-Meta-App</span>: <span class="pl-s">domain-wide-forward-auth-catch-all</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Individual Application (forwardAuth) manual</h3><a id="user-content-individual-application-forwardauth-manual" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Individual Application (forwardAuth) manual" href="#individual-application-forwardauth-manual"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Maybe you don't want to use the wizard, though I'm not sure why.  So here's how you can do it without the Wizard.</p>
<p dir="auto">An Application specific Forward Auth configuration will allow different authentication flows to be selected and not disrupt the default domain authentication flow. For example the default domain authentication flow allows a user to authentication with Authentik using username/password only. An application specific could be used for app with additional security ie an OTP, or local networks only, etc.. In most cases the default authentication flow will serve most homelab uses.</p>
<p dir="auto">As of version 2022.07.03 authentik still requires <code>/outpost.goauthentik.io/</code> to be routed <strong>IF USING INDIVIDUAL APPLICATIONS INSTEAD OF A SINGLE DOMAIN WIDE CATCH-ALL</strong>. At the end of July 2022 <code>BeryJu</code> has an upcoming fix that should remove the below label.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><em>Note: This does not seem to be required on everyone's setup. Individual Application forwardAuth does not work on mine without this label. I recommend you check your setup both with this label.</em></p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/goauthentik/authentik/pull/3151" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/goauthentik/authentik/pull/3151/hovercard">"providers/proxy: no exposed urls #3151"</a> This PR greatly simplifies the Forward auth setup for traefik and envoy. It'll remove the requirement <code>/outpost.goauthentik.io</code> to be openly accessible, which makes setup easier and decreases attack surface.</p>
</div>
<p dir="auto">This label is applied to the <code>authentik_server</code> container.  Even if you don't use individual applications, keep this label just in case you DO in the future!</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    labels:
      - &quot;traefik.enable=true&quot;
      ## Individual Application forwardAuth regex (catch any subdomain using individual application forwardAuth)  
      - &quot;traefik.http.routers.authentik-output-rtr.rule=HostRegexp(`{subdomain:[a-z0-9-]+}.${DOMAINNAME}`) &amp;&amp; PathPrefix(`/outpost.goauthentik.io/`)&quot;"><pre>    labels:
      - <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>traefik.enable=true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span># Individual Application forwardAuth regex (catch any subdomain using individual application forwardAuth)  </span>
      - <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>traefik.http.routers.authentik-output-rtr.rule=HostRegexp(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>{subdomain:[a-z0-9-]+}.<span class="pl-smi">${DOMAINNAME}</span><span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>) &amp;&amp; PathPrefix(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>/outpost.goauthentik.io/<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Provider Creation (Individual Application) - Manual</h4><a id="user-content-provider-creation-individual-application---manual" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Provider Creation (Individual Application) - Manual" href="#provider-creation-individual-application---manual"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In the Admin Interface, go to:<br>
2. Applications<br>
3. Providers<br>
4. Create</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/manual_create_p.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/manual_create_p.png" alt="manual-create-p" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Select <code>Proxy Provider</code><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/m-pp.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/m-pp.png" alt="m-pp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Use the following settings:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Name: <code>whoami-individual provider</code></li>
<li>Authentication Flow: <code>empty</code><br>
<em>This is user choice, I recommend getting the basics setup and THEN modifying authentication flow for the catch all</em></li>
<li>Authorization Flow: <code>default-provider-authorization-explicit-consent (Authorize Application)</code></li>
<li>Type: <code>Forward auth (single application)</code><br>
<em>Single Application is where we change it up!</em></li>
<li>External Host: <code>https://whoami-individual.domain.tld</code></li>
<li>Token Validity: <code>hours=24</code><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/m-pp-settings.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/m-pp-settings.png" alt="m-pp-settings" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">After hitting Finish it will show that it's not bound to an Application:
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/unbound-provider.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/unbound-provider.png" alt="unbound-provider" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Application Creation (Individual Application) - Manual</h4><a id="user-content-application-creation-individual-application---manual" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Application Creation (Individual Application) - Manual" href="#application-creation-individual-application---manual"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In the Admin Interface, go to:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Applications</li>
<li>Applications</li>
<li>Create</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/m-app.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/m-app.png" alt="m-app" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Name: <code>whoami-individual application</code></li>
<li>Slug: <code>whoami-individual-application</code></li>
<li>Group: <code>empty</code></li>
<li>Provider: <code>whoami-individual provider</code><br>
<em><strong>This is where you bind it to the previously created provider!</strong></em></li>
<li>Backchannel Providers: <code>empty</code></li>
<li>Policy Engine Mode: <code>any</code></li>
<li>UI Settings
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Launch URL: <code>https://whoami-individual.domain.tld</code><br>
<em>Since this is an individual application, specify where it is found at</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/m-app-c.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/m-app-c.png" alt="Manual-App-Create" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">After hitting Create it will show that it is now bound to the previously created provider:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/m-app-bound.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/m-app-bound.png" alt="Manual-App-Bound" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Embedded Outpost (Individual Application)</h4><a id="user-content-embedded-outpost-individual-application" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Embedded Outpost (Individual Application)" href="#embedded-outpost-individual-application"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Navigate to the Outposts screen and edit the Embedded Outpost:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Applications</li>
<li>Outposts</li>
<li>Edit the Embedded Outpost</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/embed_outpost_edit2.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/embed_outpost_edit2.png" alt="embed-outpost-2" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Highlight any application you want the outpost to be able to provide for. In this case Highlight <code>whoami-individual application</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><em><strong>BEFORE HIGHLIGHT</strong></em><br>
Notice that BEFORE highlighting and adding to Selected Applications, it still has only the <code>Domain Wide Forward Auth Catch All</code> rule in Selected Applications:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/before_add_2nd.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/before_add_2nd.png" alt="before-add-2nd" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><em><strong>AFTER HIGHLIGHT</strong></em><br>
This will include both the domain wide (catch all) and the individual application bound to this outpost.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/after_add_2nd.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/after_add_2nd.png" alt="after-add-2nd" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">After hitting Update the Outpost page will show that the embedded outpost now has both providers bound to it:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/outpost_with2.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/outpost_with2.png" alt="outpost-with-2" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Individual Application Test/Validation</h3><a id="user-content-individual-application-testvalidation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Individual Application Test/Validation" href="#individual-application-testvalidation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Now that the individual application rule is in place, validate it using the already running <code>whoami-individual</code> container created:</p>
<p dir="auto">Navigate to <code>whoami-individual.domain.tld</code> and it will immediately redirect you to Authentik to login:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/fa_splash2.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/fa_splash2.png" alt="fa-splash" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Sign in with your username or email address initially created. After inputting username &amp; password, it should show you the "Redirecting" screen prior to actual redirection:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/whoami-indiv.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/whoami-indiv.png" alt="whoami-all" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>X-Authentik-Meta-App</code> will contain information about the specific Application used to get here. Notice that this matches the <code>slug</code> previously created.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="X-Authentik-Meta-App: whoami-individual-application"><pre><span class="pl-ent">X-Authentik-Meta-App</span>: <span class="pl-s">whoami-individual-application</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">(Optional) New User Creation</h2><a id="user-content-optional-new-user-creation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: (Optional) New User Creation" href="#optional-new-user-creation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Inside the Admin Interface do the following steps to create an additional user:</p>
<ol dir="auto">

<li>Users</li>
<li>Create</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/user_create1.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/user_create1.png" alt="user-create-1" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Fill in the required information:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/account_create_info.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/account_create_info.png" alt="account-create-info" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">(Optional) Add user to Administrator/Superuser Group</h2><a id="user-content-optional-add-user-to-administratorsuperuser-group" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: (Optional) Add user to Administrator/Superuser Group" href="#optional-add-user-to-administratorsuperuser-group"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">(Optional) Change user password</h2><a id="user-content-optional-change-user-password" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: (Optional) Change user password" href="#optional-change-user-password"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Yubikey</h2><a id="user-content-yubikey" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Yubikey" href="#yubikey"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Read this section before just doing it!</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://docs.goauthentik.io/docs/flow/stages/authenticator_webauthn/#authenticator-attachment" rel="nofollow">https://docs.goauthentik.io/docs/flow/stages/authenticator_webauthn/#authenticator-attachment</a></p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p dir="auto">To prevent locking yourself out and having to start over by deleting your postgres database, create a backup administrator (as done above) or work on a non-administrator account.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto">If you are unable to perform the below steps, skip to the <em><strong>Force Authentication</strong></em> section below.</p>
</div>
<p dir="auto"><em><strong>Recommended to Switch to standard browser / NOT Incognito.</strong></em></p>
<p dir="auto">IF you are in the <code>Admin Interface</code> navigate to the <code>User Interface</code> via the button at the top left:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/user_interface_button.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/user_interface_button.png" alt="user_interface_button" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Navigate to the <code>MFA Devices</code> screen:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Settings</li>
<li>MFA Devices</li>
<li>Enroll</li>
<li>WebAuthn device</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/settings_cog.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/settings_cog.png" alt="settings-cog" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Enrollment with Credential on Key</h3><a id="user-content-enrollment-with-credential-on-key" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Enrollment with Credential on Key" href="#enrollment-with-credential-on-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/mfa_dev.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/mfa_dev.png" alt="mfa-dev" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">During setup process, depending on your WebAuthn settings you might get prompted for a PIN:
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/webauthn-pin.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/webauthn-pin.png" alt="webauthn-pin" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">If you are unsure about this, then review the following Yubikey documentation / explanation (<a href="https://support.yubico.com/hc/en-us/articles/4402836718866-Understanding-YubiKey-PINs" rel="nofollow">https://support.yubico.com/hc/en-us/articles/4402836718866-Understanding-YubiKey-PINs</a>)</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><em>If you are being prompted for a PIN (including setting one up), and you're not sure which PIN it is, most likely it is your YubiKey's FIDO2 PIN.</em></p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Now complete the WebAuthn Setup:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/webauthn1.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/webauthn1.png" alt="webauthn1" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Hit next and you'll see that you are about to setup your key:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/webauthn2.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/webauthn2.png" alt="webauthn2" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<hr>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/choose_path.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/choose_path.png" alt="choose-path" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-caution" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-stop mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M4.47.22A.749.749 0 0 1 5 0h6c.199 0 .389.079.53.22l4.25 4.25c.141.14.22.331.22.53v6a.749.749 0 0 1-.22.53l-4.25 4.25A.749.749 0 0 1 11 16H5a.749.749 0 0 1-.53-.22L.22 11.53A.749.749 0 0 1 0 11V5c0-.199.079-.389.22-.53Zm.84 1.28L1.5 5.31v5.38l3.81 3.81h5.38l3.81-3.81V5.31L10.69 1.5ZM8 4a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v3.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-3.5A.75.75 0 0 1 8 4Zm0 8a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Caution</p><p dir="auto">By performing the setup like this, it asks to create a credential on the Yubikey device itself. If you want to make it where it does NOT create the credential itself skip setup for now and go to the <code>Modify WebAuthn Credential Creation Location</code> section where I will show how to change the save credential to key option. After changing that option, you can revisit setup.</p>
</div>
<p dir="auto"><em><strong>STOP</strong></em> - Read the Above Caution Statement before continuing!</p>
<p dir="auto">If you're ok with creating the credential on your key, continue!</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/webauthn3.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/webauthn3.png" alt="webauthn3" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Modify WebAuthn Credential Creation Location</h3><a id="user-content-modify-webauthn-credential-creation-location" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Modify WebAuthn Credential Creation Location" href="#modify-webauthn-credential-creation-location"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In order to modify the default settings to prevent saving a credential on the Yubikey itself perform the following steps.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Go to the Admin Interface</li>
<li>Flows and Stages</li>
<li>Stages</li>
<li>Edit <code>default-authenticator-webauthn-setup</code></li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/edit_webauthn.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/edit_webauthn.png" alt="edit-webauthn" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Review the default settings:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/res_key_def.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/res_key_def.png" alt="res-key-def" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Edit the <code>Resident key requirement</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Default: <code>Preferred: The authenticator can create and store a dedicated credential, but if it doesn't that's alright too</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Unfortunately, if I try to skip the dedicated credential, I am unable to setup a Yubikey. I am going to set this option to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Modified: <code>Discouraged: The authenticator should not create a dedicated credential</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/res_key_change.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/res_key_change.png" alt="res-key-change" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">(Optional) Edit the <code>User verification</code> depending on your WebAuthn expertise.</h4><a id="user-content-optional-edit-the-user-verification-depending-on-your-webauthn-expertise" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: (Optional) Edit the User verification depending on your WebAuthn expertise." href="#optional-edit-the-user-verification-depending-on-your-webauthn-expertise"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">I am leaving it default:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Default: <code>Preferred: User verification is preferred if available, but not required</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">(Optional) Authenticator preference</h4><a id="user-content-optional-authenticator-preference" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: (Optional) Authenticator preference" href="#optional-authenticator-preference"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Authentik by default has no preference set for the Authenticator, as shown in the above picture. This can be changed to be explicitly <code>Yubikey</code> OR <code>Windows Hello/TouchID</code>. If you do not want to be prompted by Windows Hello, as shown in the Windows Hello section, then set this to <code>A "roaming" authenticator, like a YubiKey</code>.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/yubi_pref.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/yubi_pref.png" alt="yubi-pref" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Finish Registration</h4><a id="user-content-finish-registration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Finish Registration" href="#finish-registration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you chose to NOT save your key on the Yubikey like above, then scroll back up to continue the registration / finish it.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/finish_mfa_reg.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/finish_mfa_reg.png" alt="finish-mfa-reg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">(Troubleshooting) Windows Hello</h3><a id="user-content-troubleshooting-windows-hello" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: (Troubleshooting) Windows Hello" href="#troubleshooting-windows-hello"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">During Security Key enrollment, if you are interrupted by Windows Hello shown here:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/win_hello.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/win_hello.png" alt="win-hello" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Press <code>ESC</code> to continue to actual Yubikey enrollment. This only seems to happen if you have previously setup Windows Hello.</p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto">If you are prompted for a PIN that you do not know, go to the <code>Enrollment with Credential on Key</code> section for the Yubikey documentation link to address the PIN.  Optionally, you can also Force it to skip Windows Hello and go straight to the Yubikey by modifying the <code>default-authenticator-webauthn-setup</code>, as seen in the <code>(Optional) Authenticator preference</code> section above.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">(Optional) Force Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA)</h3><a id="user-content-optional-force-multi-factor-authentication-mfa" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: (Optional) Force Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA)" href="#optional-force-multi-factor-authentication-mfa"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To configure an authentication a user must be in the state that forces them to add an authentication. In order to do this, I am going to modify the default flow for authentication regarding MFA devices.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Go to the Admin Interface</li>
<li>Flows &amp; Stages</li>
<li>Stages</li>
<li>Edit <code>default-authentication-mfa-validation</code></li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/default_mfa.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/default_mfa.png" alt="default-mfa" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">The initial settings for the <code>default-authentication-mfa-validation</code> stage look like this:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/mfa-stage-defaults.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/mfa-stage-defaults.png" alt="mfa-stage-defaults" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Change the <code>Device Classes</code> to what options you want you or other users to have (by default). I am only going to <strong>REMOVE</strong> static tokens.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/no-static.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/no-static.png" alt="no-static" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Modify the <code>Not configured action</code> to <code>Force the user to configure an authenticator</code>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Default: <code>Continue</code></li>
<li>Modified: <code>Force the user to configure an authenticator</code><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/force-mfa.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/force-mfa.png" alt="force-mfa" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">After setting the <code>Not configured action</code> to <code>Force the user to configure an authenticator</code> it will unlock the <code>Configuration stages</code> options as seen above.<br>
This section, as it says right below it</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Stages used to configure Authenticator when user doesn't have any compatible devices. After this configuration Stage passes, the user is not prompted again.<br>
When multiple stages are selected, the user can choose which one they want to enroll.</p>
</blockquote>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Select: <code>default-authenticator-totp-setup (TOP Authenticator Setup Stage)</code></li>
<li>Select: <code>default-authenticator-webauthn-setup (WebAuthn Authenticator Setup Stage)</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">In order to highlight multiple, use the <code>Shift</code> key.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/mfa-selections.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/mfa-selections.png" alt="mfa-selections" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Hit <code>Update</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Open another <strong>INCOGNITO</strong> browser and navigate back to the <code>whoami-individual</code> URL or <code>authentik</code>'s URL and sign in.</p>
<p dir="auto">After entering the username/password a new window pop-up asks to select an authenticator method -- choose <code>default-authenticator-webauthn-setup</code>. The following steps should match the <strong>Yubikey</strong> section above.</p>
<p dir="auto">This will only give you this option if you did not previously register your Yubikey inside of the MFA devices.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Domain Wide (Tenet) Policies</h2><a id="user-content-domain-wide-tenet-policies" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Domain Wide (Tenet) Policies" href="#domain-wide-tenet-policies"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">View the <strong>Default</strong> Flows by going to the Admin Interface</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>System</li>
<li>Brands</li>
<li>Edit <code>authentik-default</code><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/domain-def.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/domain-def.png" alt="domain-defaults" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Expand down <code>Default flows</code><br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/blob/traefik3/images/def-flows.png"><img src="/brokenscripts/authentik_traefik/raw/traefik3/images/def-flows.png" alt="def-flows" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Notice that the <strong>DEFAULT</strong> Authentication flow is <code>default-authentication-flow (Welcome to authentik!)</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Navigate to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Flows and Stages</li>
<li>Flows</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">In order to view the default <code>default-authentication-flow</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Why does this matter?  To understand the way YOU have this identity tool setup.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Authentication default</h3><a id="user-content-authentication-default" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Authentication default" href="#authentication-default"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">By default the flow for all <strong>authentication</strong>, <code>default-authentication-flow</code>, is as follows:</p>
<section class="js-render-needs-enrichment render-needs-enrichment position-relative" data-identity="9cc50726-8ec7-4e9b-974e-9857f817c274" data-host="https://viewscreen.githubusercontent.com" data-src="https://viewscreen.githubusercontent.com/markdown/mermaid?docs_host=https%3A%2F%2Fdocs.github.com" data-type="mermaid" aria-label="mermaid rendered output container">

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Authorization defaults</h3><a id="user-content-authorization-defaults" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Authorization defaults" href="#authorization-defaults"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">There are two policies for <strong>authorization</strong>, explicit, <code>default-provider-authorization-explicit-consent</code>, and implicit, <code>default-provider-authorization-implicit-consent</code>.  By default the <strong>explicit</strong> policy is used.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Explicit</h4><a id="user-content-explicit" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Explicit" href="#explicit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Explicit, <code>default-provider-authorization-explicit-consent</code>, requires a pop-up showing that you accept your information is about to be shared with the site.  This could be your email, username or whatever you have setup.</p>
<section class="js-render-needs-enrichment render-needs-enrichment position-relative" data-identity="da5fdbc5-f6f5-4830-a55a-8fbe45f403df" data-host="https://viewscreen.githubusercontent.com" data-src="https://viewscreen.githubusercontent.com/markdown/mermaid?docs_host=https%3A%2F%2Fdocs.github.com" data-type="mermaid" aria-label="mermaid rendered output container">

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Implicit</h4><a id="user-content-implicit" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Implicit" href="#implicit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Implicit, <code>default-provider-authorization-implicit-consent</code>, means that by logging in you accept your information (email or username, etc.) will be shared with the site, do not prompt, just continue through.</p>
